{"nick":"joepie91","message":"this is what allows you to load multiple versions of the same package even if they contain stuff with the same name","date":"2019-02-05T19:20:37.009Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"shinzo","date":"2019-02-05T19:20:57.191Z","type":"join"}

{"nick":"reber","date":"2019-02-05T19:21:28.419Z","type":"join"}
